About momozzi
</div> <h3 class="text-3xl md:text-5xl font-black tracking-tighter leading-[1.1] text-neutral-900 dark:text-white break-keep">
당신의 '먹거리 고민'을 해결하는<br> <span class="text-orange-600 dark:text-orange-500">momozzi</span>입니다.
</h3> </div> <!-- 특징 카드 그리드 --> <div class="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-6"> <!-- Card 01 --> <div class="group p-8 rounded-4xl bg-white dark:bg-neutral-900 border border-neutral-200 dark:border-neutral-800 hover:border-orange-500 transition-all duration-500 shadow-sm hover:shadow-2xl hover:shadow-orange-500/10 flex flex-col gap-6"> <div class="w-12 h-12 rounded-2xl bg-orange-100 dark:bg-orange-900/30 flex items-center justify-center text-2xl group-hover:scale-110 transition-transform duration-500">
🎯
</div> <div class="flex flex-col gap-3"> <h4 class="text-lg font-black text-neutral-900 dark:text-white uppercase tracking-tighter">맞춤 매칭</h4> <p class="text-sm font-bold text-neutral-500 dark:text-neutral-400 leading-relaxed break-keep">
500개 이상의 방대한 데이터를 바탕으로 사용자의 기분과 취향에 최적화된 결과만을 엄선합니다.
</p> </div> </div> <!-- Card 02 --> <div class="group p-8 rounded-4xl bg-white dark:bg-neutral-900 border border-neutral-200 dark:border-neutral-800 hover:border-orange-500 transition-all duration-500 shadow-sm hover:shadow-2xl hover:shadow-orange-500/10 flex flex-col gap-6"> <div class="w-12 h-12 rounded-2xl bg-neutral-100 dark:bg-neutral-800 flex items-center justify-center text-2xl group-hover:scale-110 transition-transform duration-500">
🏷️
</div> <div class="flex flex-col gap-3"> <h4 class="text-lg font-black text-neutral-900 dark:text-white uppercase tracking-tighter">태그 분석</h4> <p class="text-sm font-bold text-neutral-500 dark:text-neutral-400 leading-relaxed break-keep">
맛, 식감, 요리 방식 등 세분화된 태그 시스템을 통해 당신이 진짜 원하는 맛을 정교하게 찾아냅니다.
</p> </div> </div> <!-- Card 03 --> <div class="group p-8 rounded-4xl bg-white dark:bg-neutral-900 border border-neutral-200 dark:border-neutral-800 hover:border-orange-500 transition-all duration-500 shadow-sm hover:shadow-2xl hover:shadow-orange-500/10 flex flex-col gap-6"> <div class="w-12 h-12 rounded-2xl bg-neutral-100 dark:bg-neutral-800 flex items-center justify-center text-2xl group-hover:scale-110 transition-transform duration-500">
📈
</div> <div class="flex flex-col gap-3"> <h4 class="text-lg font-black text-neutral-900 dark:text-white uppercase tracking-tighter">트렌드 분석</h4> <p class="text-sm font-bold text-neutral-500 dark:text-neutral-400 leading-relaxed break-keep">
대중적인 인기 순위와 랭킹 시스템을 도입하여 가장 사랑받는 먹거리 정보를 투명하게 공유합니다.
</p> </div> </div> <!-- Card 04 --> <div class="group p-8 rounded-4xl bg-white dark:bg-neutral-900 border border-neutral-200 dark:border-neutral-800 hover:border-orange-500 transition-all duration-500 shadow-sm hover:shadow-2xl hover:shadow-orange-500/10 flex flex-col gap-6"> <div class="w-12 h-12 rounded-2xl bg-neutral-100 dark:bg-neutral-800 flex items-center justify-center text-2xl group-hover:scale-110 transition-transform duration-500">
🏠
</div> <div class="flex flex-col gap-3"> <h4 class="text-lg font-black text-neutral-900 dark:text-white uppercase tracking-tighter">상황별 추천</h4> <p class="text-sm font-bold text-neutral-500 dark:text-neutral-400 leading-relaxed break-keep">
혼밥, 야식, 홈파티 등 다양한 상황에 적합한 메뉴를 카테고리별로 쉽고 빠르게 탐색하세요.
</p> </div> </div> <!-- Card 05 --> <div class="group p-8 rounded-4xl bg-white dark:bg-neutral-900 border border-neutral-200 dark:border-neutral-800 hover:border-orange-500 transition-all duration-500 shadow-sm hover:shadow-2xl hover:shadow-orange-500/10 flex flex-col gap-6"> <div class="w-12 h-12 rounded-2xl bg-neutral-100 dark:bg-neutral-800 flex items-center justify-center text-2xl group-hover:scale-110 transition-transform duration-500">
🛒
</div> <div class="flex flex-col gap-3"> <h4 class="text-lg font-black text-neutral-900 dark:text-white uppercase tracking-tighter">스마트 쇼핑</h4> <p class="text-sm font-bold text-neutral-500 dark:text-neutral-400 leading-relaxed break-keep">
상세 특징 확인부터 바로 구매까지 연결되는 원스톱 서비스로 당신의 시간을 획기적으로 줄여줍니다.
</p> </div> </div> <!-- Card 06 --> <div class="group p-8 rounded-4xl bg-white dark:bg-neutral-900 border border-neutral-200 dark:border-neutral-800 hover:border-orange-500 transition-all duration-500 shadow-sm hover:shadow-2xl hover:shadow-orange-500/10 flex flex-col gap-6"> <div class="w-12 h-12 rounded-2xl bg-neutral-100 dark:bg-neutral-800 flex items-center justify-center text-2xl group-hover:scale-110 transition-transform duration-500">
